STZAL, RGYAL DBANG MCHOG GI BKAS BSKUL MA MDZAD PA LTAR, LHA
MO'I GSER SKYEMS DANG THA 'OG CHOS SKYONG LA MCHOD GTOR 'BUL
TSUL BCAS BKA' RTZOM GNANG, BKA' BLON LHAN RGYAS

NAS PHEBS RDZONGS KYI DNGOS PO BSTABS, SMON LAM CHEN MO GROL BA
NAS SKABS SNGA PHYIR RGYAL BA YAB SRAS ZUNG GI ZHABS BRTAN DANG
MTHA' DBUS KYI 'GRO BA RNAMS BDE THABS SU DMIGS SER 'BRAS DGE
GSUM, PHUR BU LCOG ,AUR GE GRVA

TSANG; RME RU, RNAM RGYAL GRVA TSANG, BKRA SHIS LJONGS BCAS PAR
MANG JA STZAL TE GZUNGS BSDUS, GSER 'OD, BRGYAD STONG PA, SGROL
MA, GDUGS SHER BZLOG BCAS, CHOS SRUNG GI BSKANG BA, 'BYUNG BZHI
GTOR MA SOGS RGYA CHER BSGRUB,

LA MO'I DGON KHAG GSUM DU ZLA CHOS RER TSANGS BZHI DRAG GI
BSKANG GSO, DGA' LDAN CHOS RGYAL GYI SKU MDUN DU DGE SLONG
BRGYAD GRVAS ZLA BA GCIG GI RING CHOS RGYAL GYI BSKANG GSO MDZAD
RGYU'I DGOS CHA DANG, PHYAG MTSAN THOD DBYUG ZHAGS PA

BCAS PHUL, TSES NYER GSUM LA NO MON HAN RIN PO CHE DANG, PHUR BU
LCOG SPRUL PA'I SKU LA MGON PO'I RJES GNANG STZAL, DE RJES YAB
SRAS LHAN RGYAS SHING CHIBS BSGYUR DANG NYE BA BCAS YAB SRAS
PHAN TSUN THUGS 'PHRANG BA'I RNAM PA CHES

CHER MDZAD PAS DRUNG NA 'KHOD PA RNAMS KYANG DAD PA'I BA SPU
GA-YO ZHING MCHIM 'KHRUGS PAR GYUR, SKYABS 'JUG GI SNYAN 'DEBS
KYANG PHAN TSUN ZHU RES MDZAD, DE LTAR YUL DBUS PHO BRANG CHEN
PO PO TA LAR ZHABS ZUNG BKOD DE ZAB PA DANG

@032A *, ,RGYA CHE BA'I CHOS BKA' YID BZHIN GYI NOR BU'I GAN
MDZOD KYIS RGYAL DBANG MCHOG GI THUGS KYI GRU RDZINGS NI YONGS
SU BKANG, 'PHRIN LAS KYI SBRIN LAS GTONG BA'I CHAR CHEN PO PHAB
STE, DGE 'DUN GNYIS SKYES BYE

BA'I TSOGS NI TSIM PAR MDZAD, DAM PA'I CHOS KYI NYAL 'GRO NYIN
BZHIN 'BAB PAS DON GNYER RE BA'I RDZING BU NI YONGS SU KHENGS,
BSDU BA'I DNGOS PO BZHI DANG 'BREL BA'I RNAM PAR DKAR BA'I MDZAD
PAS GDUL BYA MTHA' YAS PA RNAMS

THAR PA DANG THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA'I GRONG KHYER DU 'JUG PA'I LAM
BZANG PO GSAL BAR MDZAD DO, ,TSOGS GNYIS BYE BAS NYER BSKRUN
ZHABS SOR RDUL, ,GANG DU LHUNG BA'I DPAL LDAN NOR 'DZIN MAR,
,SRID PA'I PHUN TSOGS 'KHRI SHING RGYAS

PA'I RTZER, ,DAM CHOS GSER GYI SNYEMS CI YANG DUD, ,PHYOGS KYI
'KHOR LO'I GDONG PAR 'PHRIN LAS KYI, ,NGO MTSAR 'OD RIS GSAR DU
'PHOS PA YIS, ,RTZOD LDAN RGUD PA KUN LA 'JIGS STER BA, ,KHYOD
KYIS 'GRO 'DI SRID MTHA'I BAR DU

SKYONG; ;DE NAS TSES NYER BZHI'I NYIN PHO BRANG CHEN PO PO TA
LA NAS GTZANG DU CHIBS KHA BSGYUR, SRID SKYONG AER TE NI NO MON
HAN, LI'U AAM PAN DANG HING AAM PAN, BKA' BLON BZHI SOGS RGYA
BOD KYI MI DRAG RNAMS KYIS MTSON PA'I

SER SKYA RTA BA BRGYA PHRAG MANG PO'I CHIBS SKYEL DANG BCAS GSOL
TSIGS KHANG DU THAB 'DZIN SAR ZHABS ZUNG BKOD, 'KHRUNGS LHA'I
RTEN LA GSOL MCHOD MDZAD, CHIBS SKYEL BA PHYIR LOG RNAMS LA GO
BABS DANG BSTUN PA'I GNANG

@032B CHA STZAL, 'DI NAS BZUNG GDAN SA CHEN PO'I BAR PHEBS LAM
YUL GRU RNAMS SU LHA SDE KHAG GI BLA MA LAS SNE, RDZONG GZHIS
KYI SNE MO BA, SGER LDING SOGS KYI CHIBS BSU SKYEL DANG, DGE
'DUN RNAMS NAS SER SBRENG, MI SDE'I BRO GZHAS

SOGS RTZED SNA'I GZIGS 'BUL, DAR 'PHYAR, PA SANGS SNA'I DUD
SPRIN RNAMS BAR MA CHED DU BSTAR ZHING CHIBS SKYEL BA SOGS DE
DAG RNAMS LA GNANG CHA DANG SKYE BO MANG POR PHYAG DBANG STZAL,
MTSAN NYID GLING KHAR 'BRAS SPUNGS NAS BSNYEN

BKUR DANG DNGOS 'BUL BSTABS, BLA MA LAS SNE RNAMS LA MJAL KHA
DANG BKA' 'DRI GNANG, STOD LUNG SGANG DU BZHUGS ZHAG THOG RGYAL
DBANG MCHOG GI SKU'I KHU BO RJE DRUNG BLO BZANG PHUN TSOGS NAS
DKAR SPRO SOGS ZHABS TOG BZAB CING DNGOS

'BUL SBAM MTHO BTEG ,LI'U AAM PAN DANG BKA' BLON RAGS KHA SHAG
,HOR KHANG GSAR JA SAG ,MDA' DPON PHU LUNG PA, BKA' SHAG MGRON
DRUNG SOGS LA DNGOS SKYES GNANG, BLO GLING BLA MA 'JAM DBYANGS
PHUN TSOGS KYI SKU SKYE'I GTZUG PHUD

BZHES TE BLO BZANG BKRA SHIS ZHES PA'I MING STZAL, GZHUNG 'BUL
GSOL CHAS SBAM MTHO SNGAR BZHIN BSTAR THOG NAS PHEBS SKYEL SNE
SHAN MGRON GNYER ZHA LU MKHAN PO DANG, CHIBS DBON BKRAS MTHONG
BA, DGA' LDAN SPYI GNYER, GZHUNG

DREL MGO PO KHAG BCAS LA ZUR GSOS STZAL, DE'I PHYI NYIN SNGA DRO
SRID SKYONG AER TE NI NO MON HAN LA LUGS GNYIS LAS BRTZAMS PA'I
BKA' MCHID PHEBS, DPON GA-YOG TSANG MAR DNGOS SKYES BZANG PO
STZAL, SNYE THANG 'OR TU SGROL MA

@033A *, ,SOGS RTEN RNAMS LA SNYAN SHAL MCHOD 'BUL MDZAD, RIGS
PA'I 'BYUNG GNAS STAG TSANG RAB STOD PA'I DGE 'DUN RNAMS LA
BYANG CHUB LAM GYI SGRON MA'I LUNG STZAL, BSE KHRAB PA'I MCHOD
PHRIN GNANG ZHING SKU MKHAR

LA DAR GYI COD BAN 'DZUGS PA MDZAD, GNAM DU BZHUGS ZHAG MDZAD
NAS TSES NYER DRUG LA CHIBS KHA BSGYUR TE LJANG SMAD DU SNE SHAN
GA-YUL KHA CHOS MDZAD NAS DNGOS 'BYOR GYI MCHOD SPRIN SPROS
SHING GRA SGRIG PA ZHOL SDE PA SNANG DKAR BA DANG

ZHOL DRUNG GSUM BCAS LA GNANG CHA STZAL, BKRA SHIS RTZER BZHUGS
ZHAG SAR LCAGS ZAM SPRUL SKU DANG GA RE LHA BA SO SO DKAR SPRO'I
THOG DNGOS 'BUL BTEG ,BKA' BLON JA SAG BLA MA 'DI NAS PHYIR
'BYON RGYUR RGYAL DBANG MCHOG LA 'TSAMS

ZHU'I KHA BTAGS 'BUL RGYU GNANG, KHONG NGO GA-YOG LA GNANG SKYES
STZAL, DE'I PHYI NYIN CHU BO RI'I GRU SA BYANG DU GSOL TSIGS SAR
CHIBS SKYEL DU BYON PA SKU'I KHU BO NYID DANG LHA KLU DGA' TSAL
GYI SRAS SKU MCHED LA BKA' SLOB DANG GNANG CHA BZANG

PO BSTAR, CHOS 'KHOR YANG RTZE BA DANG THAR PA GLING BA SO SO
NAS DKAR SBRO'I THOG DNGOS 'BUL DANG, CHU SHUR RDZONG YONG,

SPROS, PHEBS GRUR DAR GYI COD PAN DANG, MGO BYED, MNYAN

PA; 'UL MI SOGS LA GNANG CHA MDO MI DMA' BA STZAL, GSHAM SMAD DU

@033B GSHONG RA BA SMAD PA, BDE CHEN CHOS 'KHOR BA BCAS KYIS
DNGOS 'BYOR GYI MCHOD SBRIN SPROS RJES GONG DKAR CHOS SDE BA BCU
GCIG NAS RNGA 'CHAMS GYI GZIGS MO PHUL, TSES NYER BRGYAD KYI
NYIN PHAN LA GSHAM DU BZHUGS ZHAG SAR RGYAL DBANG

@034B GZHUNG LA TSOGS LANG MDZAD, DPAL CHOS MKHAN POS DNGOS 'BUL

RTZI'I CHU RGYUN GYI LUNG GNANG, GZIMS CHUNG DU DKAR SPRO DANG
GUNG STON SOGS BSNYEN BKUR BZANG PO BSTABS,

GA-YON DU BSIL GRIB KYI DON DU BTZUGS PA'I SHING LJON PA'I SDONG
PO TSAR DU DANG RA BA'I GZHUNG LAM NAS BYON, RIM GYIS LO CI CHOG
KO ZHES PAR GUNG DRO DANG, TA ME LA YUN

SHAN ZHES PA'I GZIMS KHANG DU ZHAG BZHUGS MDZAD, DER PHO BRANG
NANG NAS HONG WANG DANG, AA GUS AAM PAN, YUNG HE GUNG, TZAN DAN
JO BO, SHA RA SU MI SOGS NANG GI DGON PA RNAMS KYI BLA MA, LAS
SNE SOGS RTA PA STONG PHRAG LA NYE

BA 'BYOR PAR PHYAG DBANG DANG GNANG CHA STZAL, TSES GNAM GANG GI
NYIN KHO YU SHAN DU GSOL JA BTEG ,NANG SHI SO ZHES PAR GUNG DRO
BAB, LANG KVA SU ZHES PA'I GZIMS KHANG DU ZHAG BZHUGS GNANG,
PHEBS BSU BA MIS CHING WANG DPON

GA-YOG MANG PO 'BYOR TE DNGOS 'BUL BSTAR ZHING PHYAG DBANG JA
GRAL BKA' 'DRI GNANG SKYES BCAS STZAL, ZLA BA DGU PA'I TSES GCIG
GI NYIN DE NAS CHIBS KHA BSGYUR TE CHING KH'A BA PHU ZER BA'I
GZIMS KHANG DU GSOL JA BTEG ,'KHOR

@224A *, ,CHOGS STONG PHRAG DU MAS BSKOR TE TZI NA'I YUL GRU
CHEN PO'I DBUS SA GZHI KHOD SNYOMS SHING SHIN TU RGYA CHE BA,
'BYOR BA RGYAS SHING LO LEGS PA, SKYE BO MANG POS YONGS SU GANG
BA'I RGYAL KHAB CHEN PO'I NYE 'DABS SU,

MTSAN DPE'I RGYAL MTSAN MJAL BAR 'ONGS PA'I KHRO MA CHEN PO DMAR
NAG TU 'KHYIL BA'I DBUS GSHAGS TE PHEBS PA NA, LHA SRAS DRUG PA,
NANG GI AA MA PAN DU MA, DGON KHAG RNAMS KYI BLA MA LAS SNE SOGS
SER SKYA MANG PO DANG,

KHRIMS LAS KYI RU MTSON, GDUGS, RGYAL MTSAN, BA DAN, LAS DAR SNA
TSOGS LAG TU THOGS PA'I DMAG MI RTA PA STONG PHRAG BRGAL BA'I
CHIBS BSU DANG, DGE 'DUN GRANGS MED PAS CHOS GOS SNAM SBYAR
GSOL, DUR SMRIG GI RTAGS

KYIS MDZES PAR BKLUBS SHING SPOS PHOR THOGS PAS SNA DRANGS GDUGS
DANG, RGYAL MTSAN DANG, BA DAN THOGS PA, RNGA BO CHE DANG, DUNG
DANG, DUNG DKAR DANG, RDZA RNGA DANG, 'KHAR RNGA DANG, PI WANG
RGYUD GCIG PA DANG, SGRA BRNYAN DANG, GLING BU

DANG; RGYA GRING DANG, MDO DAR SOGS KYI ROL MO DANG, ME TOG
DANG, PHRENG BA DANG, BYUG PA DANG, PHYE MA PHUR MA SOGS MCHOD
RDZAS SNA TSOGS BA THOGS PA'I SER SBRENG GI SA MDUN BSUS TE
RGYAL DBANG LNGA PA CHEN PO'I BZHUGS GNAS KYANG MDZAD

PA LHA KHANG SER POR GRAGS PA'I KHANG BZANG SKABS GSUM DBANG
PO'I PHO BRANG LA 'GRAN BZOD PA'I NANG DU MI 'JIGS SENG GE'I
KHRIL ZHABS SKYES KYI PADMO NYE BAR BKOD DO, ,STOBS BCU'I CHA
SHAS YONGS GANG CHU SHEL DBANG, ,GRANGS MED

@224B ZHAM RING RGYU SKAR TSOGS DANG BCAS, ,GRONG DANG GRONG
KHYER RNAM MANG RIM BRGYUD DE, ,RGYAL KHAB CHEN PO'I 'GRAM DU
NYE BAR BYON, ,DE TSE SNA TSOGS MTSON CHA THOGS PA YI, ,DMAG MI
STONG PHRAG MANG PO'I CHIBS BSU DANG, ,DUR SMRIG 'DZIN PA'I

TSOGS KYIS MDUN BSUS TE, ,YID 'PHROG LHA KHANG SER POR ZHABS
ZUNG BKOD, ,DE TSE MTSAN DPE'I DKYIL 'KHOR SNANG BRNYAN NI,
,'DREN BYED ME LONG DANG BAR 'PHOS PA YI, ,DAD LDAN SKYE BO
BGRANG DU YAS PA KUN, ,SMIN GROL BDUD RTZI'I

DBAL GYIS MYOS PAR GYUR, ,DE NAS GONG MA'I MDZOD NAS GZHIS LEN
GYI STON CHEN DANG ZLOS GAR GYI RTZED MO SOGS MCHOD SPRIN RGYA
CHEN PO SPROS, DE RJES YANG THOG GZIMS CHUNG DU ZHABS ZUNG BKOD,
LCANG SKYA RDO RJE 'CHANG MJAL DU BYON

BAR LUGS GNYIS LAS BRTZAMS PA'I GSUNG 'PHROS SMAR, PHO BRANG DU
BZHUGS RING SNE SHAN DU BSKOS PA'I CING AAM PAN YAB SRAS NAS
DKAR SPRO DANG DNGOS 'BUL BSTAR ZHING JA GRAL GYI THOG DGYES
PA'I BKA' MCHID KYANG MDZAD, TSES

GNYIS KYI NYIN LHA SRAS DRUG PA NAS ZHABS TOG BA SNYEN BSKUR
GZABS, YUN RING TZAM BZHUGS NAS GSUNG GLENG MDZAD, SNGON DU
PHEBS BZHUGS GANG GNANG GI SAR LHA SRAS NAS GANG CI'I THUGS KHUR
BZHES PA BKA' DRIN CHE ZHES NANG

MDZOD KHA BTAGS, SKU BRNYAN, SPOS DANG SNAM BU SOGS PHUL TE
MNYES PAR BYAS, SBYAN GA-YOS MKHAN PO JA SAG GRAGS PA PHUN TSOGS
NAS DNGOS 'BUL BTEG STE RGYAL MO RONG LA 'GRO RGYUR BAR CHAD MI
'BYUNG BA'I SKYABS 'JUG ZHUS,

@225A *, ,JA GRAL GYI THOG BKA' 'DRI DANG GNANG SKYES STZAL TE
'PHRAL YUN DU SMAN PA'I ZHAL TA GNANG, LHA KHANG SER PO'I BLA
GRVA SPYI SO NAS DKAR SPRO DANG MAndAL BCAS PHUL, DGON KHAG
RNAMS KYI BLA MA LAS SNE GRVA MANG RNAMS

DANG; DPON PO CHE CHUNG SOGS RGYA SOGS GI MJAL BA STONG PHRAG DU
MAR PHYAG DBANG STZAL, TSES GSUM GYI NYIN LHA KHANG SER PO NAS
CHIBS KHA BSGYUR TE PA'I CING NAS NUB BYANG MTSAMS SU YO MI YAN
ZHES PAR SKYED MOS TSAL GYI PHO BRANG CHEN PAR

RJE NYID DANG LHA SRAS DRUG PA, LCANG SKYA RDO RJE 'CHANG, AAM
PAN RNAMS BCAS PHEBS PAR YO MI YAN GYI NYE 'DABS SU MAN JU'I LHA
KHANG YOD PA DER ZHABS SEN BKOD DE RTEN RNAMS KYI DRUNG DU YAN
LAG BDUN PA DANG MCHOD 'BUL SNYAN SHAL BCAS

BKRA SHIS KYI ME TOG GTOR, DE SKABS ZHE HOR NAS GONG MA CHEN POS
RJE NYID LA SKU'I 'TSAMS ZHU DANG, RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD MKHYEN
PAR STZOL RGYU'I 'JA' SA DANG GSER YIG GI 'CHAR GZHI ZIN BRIS
BCAS LHA SRAS BRGYUD GNANG 'DUG PA

LCANG SKYA RDO RJE 'CHANG NAS BOD SKAD DU BSGYUR TE ZHU BA GNANG
SONG BAR THUGS SHIN TU DGYES TE GONG MA CHEN POR SKU'I 'TSAMS
ZHU DANG, KHYAD PAR DU 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS GONG MA BDAG PO CHEN PO
NAS GNAM 'OG SA STENG GI BSTAN 'GRO SPYI DANG KHYAD

PAR NYIS NUB PHYOGS KYI BSTAN 'GRO THAMS CAD DUS DANG RNAM PA
KUN TU THUGS RJE MU MTHA' MA MCHIS SHING BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA'I
BKA' DRIN CHEN POS BSKYANGS DANG SKYONG BZHIN PA'I THOG DA LAM
RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA CHEN POR

NYID DU SNGA PHYI BSNGOMS DNGUL RKYANG SRANG CHIG KHRI BZHI
STENG DRUG BRGYA BCU GSUM DANG ZHO GANG, SRANG LNGA SUM BRGYA
DRUG CU RE GNYIS RTZIS KYI DNGOS PO SNA TSOGS, GTZANG RONG

KHUL GRUB MTHA' RIS MED DANG, MNGA' RIS DGON KHAG BCAS TSANG MAR
KHYON GSER ZHO BCU GSUM, DNGUL DKAR SRANG DGU ,tAM SRANG CHIG
KHRI BRGYAD STONG LNGA BRGYA SO BDUN DANG, SRANG BZHI KHRI LNGA
STONG BDUN BRGYA BZHI BCU ZHE BDUN RTZIS KYI

DNGOS PO SNA TSOGS, DBUS PHYOGS SU'ANG, RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD
MKHYEN PA CHEN POR SNGA PHYIR PHUL BA KHYON BSNGOMS GSAR ZHO
NYIS BRGYA SUM CU, DNGUL DKAR SRANG LNGA STONG BRGYAD BRGYA DANG
NYI SHU RTZA LNGA, tAM SRANG BA RGYAD BRGYA LNGA BCU,

SRANG CHIG KHRI NYIS STONG DGU BRGYA RE DGU'I RTZIS KYI DNGOS PO
SNA TSOGS, KHRI CHEN NO MON HAN DANG, YONGS 'DZIN RIN PO CHE,
PHUR BU LCOG SPRUL SKU SOGS DANG, SNGON PHEBS RDZONG 'BUL MI
BKA' BLON SOGS BCAS PAR KHYON BSNGOMS
